OTT_great_game = {
	TUR_establish_rk_ICE = {
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
	
		
			highlight_states = {
				highlight_state_targets = {
							state = 100
	
				}
				highlight_color_while_active = 3
				highlight_color_before_active = 2
			}
	
		available = {
			100 = { owner = { OR = { original_tag = TUR is_subject_of = TUR } } }
		}
	
		fire_only_once = yes
	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5
		}
		complete_effect = {
			release = ICE
			ICE = {
				every_core_state = {
					remove_core_of = ICE
				}
			}
			100 = { add_core_of = ICE }
	
			ICE = { 
				every_core_state = {
				  limit = {
					AND = {
					  NOT = { 
						is_core_of = TUR
					  }
					  OR = {
						is_owned_by = TUR
						OWNER = { is_subject_of = TUR} 
					  }
					}
				  }
				  transfer_state_to = ICE
				}
			  }
			ICE = { 
				set_cosmetic_tag = OTT_ICE_OCC
				load_focus_tree = generic_focus            
	
				set_popularities = {
					syndicalist = 5
					social_democrat = 5
					social_liberal = 0
					market_liberal = 0
					social_conservative = 20
					authoritarian_democrat = 50
					paternal_autocrat = 10
					national_populist = 10
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					name = "Iceland Vilayet"
					long_name = "Iceland Vilayet"
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					name = "Iceland Vilayet"
					long_name = "Iceland Vilayet"
				}
	
				TUR = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = ICE
						autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
					}
				}
	
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
